═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ // SONS (Web Audio API) // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ let _ctx=null; function getCtx(){if(!_ctx)try{_ctx=new(window.AudioContext||window.webkitAudioContext)();}catch(e){}return _ctx;} function playNote(freq,start,dur,vol=0.25,type='sine'){ const ctx=getCtx();if(!ctx)return; const o=ctx.createOscillator(),g=ctx.createGain(); o.type=type;o.frequency.value=freq; g.gain.setValueAtTime(0,ctx.currentTime+start); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol,ctx.currentTime+start+0.01); g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001,ctx.currentTime+start+dur); o.connect(g);g.connect(ctx.destination); o.start(ctx.currentTime+start);o.stop(ctx.currentTime+start+dur+0.05); } function sfx(type){ if(type==='click'){playNote(600,0,0.06,0.15,'square');} else if(type==='done'){playNote(523,0,0.1);playNote(659,0.12,0.1);playNote(784,0.24,0.18);} else if(type==='easy'){[523,659,784,1047].forEach((f,i)=playNote(f,i*.12,.18,.25));} else if(type==='ok'){[440,554,659,880].forEach((f,i)=playNote(f,i*.13,.18,.22));} else if(type==='hard'){[330,0,294,0,262].forEach((f,i)={if(f)playNote(f,i*.15,.18,.2,'sawtooth');});} else if(type==='fanfare'){ const m=[523,523,523,415,523,622,415,523,659],d=[.18,.18,.18,.14,.14,.38,.18,.18,.48]; let t=0;m.forEach((f,i)={playNote(f,t,d[i],.28);t+=d[i]+.02;}); } } // rendu bindEvents(); } function buildNav(t,col){ const tabs=[ {k:'accueil',i:'🏠',l:t.accueil}, {k:'programme',i:'📋',l:t.programme}, {k:'seance',i:'💪',l:t.seance}, {k:'stats',i:'📊',l:t.stats}, {k:'profil',i:'👤',l:t.profil}, ]; return tabs.map(tab=`
